\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
Lock-\/free skip-\/list set (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu}%
 The implementation of well-\/known probabilistic data structure called skip-\/list invented by W.\+Pugh in his papers\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}1989\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh Skip Lists\+: \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Probabilistic Alternative to Balanced Trees
\item \mbox{[}1990\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Skip \doxylink{class_list}{List} Cookbook
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} skip-\/list is a probabilistic data structure that provides expected logarithmic time search without the need of rebalance. The skip-\/list is a collection of sorted linked list. Nodes are ordered by key. Each node is linked into a subset of the lists. Each list has a level, ranging from 0 to 32. The bottom-\/level list contains all the nodes, and each higher-\/level list is a sublist of the lower-\/level lists. Each node is created with a random top level (with a random height), and belongs to all lists up to that level. The probability that a node has the height 1 is 1/2. The probability that a node has the height N is 1/2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} N (more precisely, the distribution depends on an random generator provided, but our generators have this property).

The lock-\/free variant of skip-\/list is implemented according to book
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2008\mbox{]} M.\+Herlihy, N.\+Shavit "{}\+The Art of Multiprocessor Programming"{}, chapter 14.\+4 "{}\+A Lock-\/\+Free Concurrent Skiplist"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Template arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}.
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type to be stored in the list.
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ set traits, default is \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_1_1traits}{skip\+\_\+list\+::traits} for explanation.
\end{DoxyItemize}

It is possible to declare option-\/based list with \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_1_1make__traits}{cds\+::container\+::skip\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits} metafunction istead of {\ttfamily Traits} template argument. Template argument list {\ttfamily Options} of \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_1_1make__traits}{cds\+::container\+::skip\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits} metafunction are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1compare}{opt\+::compare} -\/ key comparison functor. No default functor is provided. If the option is not specified, the \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1less}{opt\+::less} is used.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1less}{opt\+::less} -\/ specifies binary predicate used for key comparison. Default is {\ttfamily std\+::less$<$\+T$>$}.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1item__counter}{opt\+::item\+\_\+counter} -\/ the type of item counting feature. Default is \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter} that is no item counting.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1memory__model}{opt\+::memory\+\_\+model} -\/ C++ memory ordering model. Can be \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1relaxed__ordering}{opt\+::v\+::relaxed\+\_\+ordering} (relaxed memory model, the default) or \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1sequential__consistent}{opt\+::v\+::sequential\+\_\+consistent} (sequentially consisnent memory model).
\item \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a95cd379ff7c8af371d88b27a2d2ff544}{skip\+\_\+list\+::random\+\_\+level\+\_\+generator} -\/ random level generator. Can be {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a441781f9787468f74a40acc289574549}{skip\+\_\+list\+::xor\+\_\+shift}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_ac136c22839c6c7c936b3bf3061c14ffd}{skip\+\_\+list\+::turbo}} or user-\/provided one. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a95cd379ff7c8af371d88b27a2d2ff544}{skip\+\_\+list\+::random\+\_\+level\+\_\+generator}} option description for explanation. Default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a7a699b46b3dbd3056df4017250caca67}{skip\+\_\+list\+::turbo32}}.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1allocator}{opt\+::allocator} -\/ allocator for skip-\/list node. Default is \doxylink{external_2libcds_2cds_2user__setup_2allocator_8h_ad5fb7e3cbe8cf24295f0ea3c165a2d82}{CDS\+\_\+\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+ALLOCATOR}.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1back__off}{opt\+::back\+\_\+off} -\/ back-\/off strategy used. If the option is not specified, the \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1backoff_a0f64f7bc371e3ad006fba5bd855d6e96}{cds\+::backoff\+::\+Default} is used.
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1stat}{opt\+::stat} -\/ internal statistics. Available types\+: \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a52900176775dc99f9e84483c4ba57498}{skip\+\_\+list\+::stat}, \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_a383c7508f659dc9d1873e3800661ef93}{skip\+\_\+list\+::empty\+\_\+stat} (the default)
\item \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1rcu__check__deadlock}{opt\+::rcu\+\_\+check\+\_\+deadlock} -\/ a deadlock checking policy. Default is \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{skip__list__set__rcu_8h}{cds/container/skip\+\_\+list\+\_\+set\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files.
\end{DoxyNote}
{\bfseries{Iterators}}

The class supports a forward iterator (\doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1b5940f7ba677154ec7a55ef24f57a4a}{iterator} and \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad533e0abfb7fceefc1e268f53b530619}{const\+\_\+iterator}). The iteration is ordered.

You may iterate over skip-\/list set items only under RCU lock. Only in this case the iterator is thread-\/safe since while RCU is locked any set\textquotesingle{}s item cannot be reclaimed.

The requirement of RCU lock during iterating means that deletion of the elements (i.\+e. \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab493c413db0b5533086aade88294d9b3}{erase}) is not possible.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The iterator object cannot be passed between threads
\end{DoxyWarning}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ rcu\_type::scoped\_lock\ destructor\ releases\ RCU\ lock\ implicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Due to concurrent nature of skip-\/list set it is not guarantee that you can iterate all elements in the set\+: any concurrent deletion can exclude the element pointed by the iterator from the set, and your iteration can be terminated before end of the set. Therefore, such iteration is more suitable for debugging purposes
\end{DoxyWarning}
The iterator class supports the following minimalistic interface\+:

Item counting policy used 

\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_abb219352dd6491a5efac6dd0b924a5fd}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!iterator@{iterator}}
\index{iterator@{iterator}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{iterator}{iterator}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_abb219352dd6491a5efac6dd0b924a5fd} 
typedef skip\+\_\+list\+::details\+::iterator$<$ typename base\+\_\+class\+::iterator $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Iterator type 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item to protect the value, the iterator contains a GC-\/specific guard + another guard is required locally for increment operator. For some GC (like as {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1gc_af0523881f089593a7559d194ee2b5dd9}{gc\+::\+HP}}), a guard is a limited resource per thread, so an exception (or assertion) "{}no free guard"{} may be thrown if the limit of guard count per thread is exceeded.
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary because it contains thread-\/private GC\textquotesingle{}s guard.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item the iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations there is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\end{DoxyWarning}

Forward iterator 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it depends on iterator of underlying {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the element the iterator points to. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a8bd4f0530a3e75b25503aa1764b85cec}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!key\_comparator@{key\_comparator}}

Clears the set (not atomic). 

The function deletes all items from the set. The function is not atomic, thus, in multi-\/threaded environment with parallel insertions this sequence

 the assertion could be raised.

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key}

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a90e363ee9bc04cbdb51689de263e0795}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

Delete {\ttfamily key} from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_erase_func}%
 The function searches an item with key {\ttfamily key}, calls {\ttfamily f} functor and deletes the item. If {\ttfamily key} is not found, the functor is not called.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} interface\+:

\end{DoxyCode}


Since the key of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}} is not explicitly specified, template parameter {\ttfamily Q} defines the key type to search in the list. The list item comparator should be able to compare the type {\ttfamily T} of list item and the type {\ttfamily Q}.

Return {\ttfamily true} if key is found and deleted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6b6f17b3f985646b6c4b57832c1b2e43}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

Since the key of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_michael_hash_set}{Michael\+Hash\+Set}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}} is not explicitly specified, template parameter {\ttfamily Q} defines the key type searching in the list. The list item comparator should be able to compare the type {\ttfamily T} of list item and the type {\ttfamily Q}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Return {\ttfamily true} if key is found and deleted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_erase_val}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afe8b3cf4ec9ba953f01966e3933aa3c9}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_aab2284cfd210c096378fe7c86157290c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The item extracted is freed automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a11b2453ae7752fee5e3ea5d0d13c36ec} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6049cfc797d21b5988e993c56cec79f9}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6049cfc797d21b5988e993c56cec79f9}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} 

Note the compare functor from {\ttfamily Traits} class\textquotesingle{} template argument should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a5d471ab598f474a25ff8fb8930960f66}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_max@{extract\_max}}
\index{extract\_max@{extract\_max}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_max()}{extract\_max()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a5d471ab598f474a25ff8fb8930960f66} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with maximal key from the set 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it, and returns the pointer to item found as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The item found is freed by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6049cfc797d21b5988e993c56cec79f9}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with maximal key from the set 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6049cfc797d21b5988e993c56cec79f9}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_ad95f728e6e8f7f78a29a16912a890bb8}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_min@{extract\_min}}
\index{extract\_min@{extract\_min}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_min()}{extract\_min()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_ad95f728e6e8f7f78a29a16912a890bb8} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the set 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns pointer to the item found as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The item extracted is freed automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts an item with minimal key from the set 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6049cfc797d21b5988e993c56cec79f9}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_acb845ff13864d403412b08dd897599d5}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}

Extracts the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afa60b186b2b18cafd7635d1a952913c3}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}

Extracts the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a11b2453ae7752fee5e3ea5d0d13c36ec}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_ab7464492eb3755390cb4bda3c82f8b30}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

\doxylink{struct_find}{Find} the {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_find_func}%
 The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that may be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_adc41967fe3db01d0c1bd08002f9f68d7}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

\doxylink{struct_find}{Find} the key {\ttfamily val} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_find_func}%
 The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily val} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily val} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily val} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor can modify both arguments.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that may be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find\_with()}{find\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a808f79ca28e33da97182166d4f0b1110} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_find_func}{find(Q\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a66ef72a211345bfbd66c064e85f18a28}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find\_with@{find\_with}}

Finds the key {\ttfamily val} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_find_func}{find(Q\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. 函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get()}{get()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a9d1806975cd89b92067fdce2a1665447} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

It is safe when a concurrent thread erases the item returned in {\ttfamily result} guarded pointer. In this case the item will be freed later by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns a {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a31532208f60434717ccd4fb8670108ea}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} object pointed to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a31532208f60434717ccd4fb8670108ea}{raw\+\_\+ptr}}.

Note the compare functor in {\ttfamily Traits} class\textquotesingle{} template argument should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a96c912a4c58cfa22165e7d7807d79b2d}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a12ec8fa6955464b19b1d77ff7a42d613}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_with()}{get\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a12ec8fa6955464b19b1d77ff7a42d613} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a31532208f60434717ccd4fb8670108ea}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily val} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a58e9f24060a29d05a775108a323b804b}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a58e9f24060a29d05a775108a323b804b} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the set.

The type {\ttfamily Q} should contain as minimum the complete key for the node. The object of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily Q}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily Q} is equal to \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afde46faa313ab4d37a57f1a492799a98}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afde46faa313ab4d37a57f1a492799a98} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the set.

The type {\ttfamily Q} should contain as minimum the complete key for the node. The object of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily Q}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily Q} is equal to \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\+\_\+type}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a4f437617d9f9b09b0fc6358b3471bbe3}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_a4f437617d9f9b09b0fc6358b3471bbe3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/fields of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_adb150efdc7e9e3347baf9d279fcc37c8}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_adb150efdc7e9e3347baf9d279fcc37c8} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/fields of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154db991dd5fa18acd55e09488d6789b}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:

Returns item count in the set 

The value returned depends on item counter type provided by {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter. If it is {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter}} this function always returns 0. Therefore, the function is not suitable for checking the set emptiness, use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aa0dd79cc12ac33825d2f3b03bb925b5c}{empty()}} member function for this purpose. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2d13d4983ae37ccf68adb5d50d95da81}\index{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!size@{size}}

std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the item 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily val} key not found in the set, then the new item created from {\ttfamily val} will be inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, if {\ttfamily val} is found, the functor {\ttfamily func} will be called with the item found.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily key} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the item has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with key equal to {\ttfamily val} already exists.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Updates the item 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If {\ttfamily val} not found in the set, then the new item created from {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with the item found. The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+:

\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is true if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is true if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already exists. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 7
